   function DetectDevice( userAgent ) {
		userAgent = userAgent.toLowerCase();
		if( RegExp( "ipod" ).test( userAgent ) || RegExp( "iphone" ).test( userAgent ) ) {
			return "phone";
		} else if( RegExp( "ipad" ).test( userAgent ) ) {
			return "tablet";
		} else if( RegExp( "android" ).test( userAgent ) ) {
			if( RegExp( "mobile" ).test( userAgent ) ) {
				return "phone";
			}
			return "tablet";
		} else if( ( RegExp( "win" ).test( userAgent ) && ! RegExp( "compatible" ).test( userAgent ) ) || RegExp( "linux" ).test( userAgent ) ){
			return "desktop";
		}
		return "unknown";
	}
	function getParameterByName( name, url ) {
		if ( "undefined" == typeof url ) {
			url = window.location.href;
		}
		name = name.replace( /[\[\]]/g, "\\$&" );
		var regex = new RegExp( "[?&]" + name + "(=([^&#]*)|&|#|$)" ),
		results = regex.exec( url );
		if ( !results ) return '';
		if ( !results[ 2 ] ) return '';
		var result = decodeURIComponent( results[2].replace(/\+/g, " ") );
		if( result.length > 15 ) return '';
		for( var x = 0; x < result.length; x++ ) {
			var charCode = result.charCodeAt( x );
			if ( ! ( 
				( 'a'.charCodeAt( 0 ) <= charCode && charCode <= 'z'.charCodeAt( 0 ) ) 
				|| ( 'A'.charCodeAt( 0 ) <= charCode && charCode <= 'z'.charCodeAt( 0 ) ) 
				|| ( '0'.charCodeAt( 0 ) <= charCode && charCode <= '9'.charCodeAt( 0 ) ) 
				) ) {
					return '';
			}
		}
		return result;
	}

     <div class="tncms-block" id="tncms-block-1911074">
      <style type="text/css">
       /* stylelint-disable declaration-no-important */
    .subscribe-button-mobile {
      display: block !important;
	  width: 95%;
    }
    .log-in-button-mobile, .log-out-button-mobile {
      display: block !important;
	  width: 95%;
          visibility:hidden;
    }
    .log-in-button-mobile a, .log-out-button-mobile a, .subscribe-button-mobile a {
		padding:15px 15px;
		font-weight:bold;
		display: block;
		font-size: 16px;
	}
      </style>
      <div class="subscribe-button-mobile">
       <a href="https://checkout.theoaklandpress.com/?g2i_source=website&amp;g2i_medium=link&amp;g2i_campaign=nav&amp;g2i_or_o=Internet&amp;g2i_or_p=nav" onclick="$(`.active-right.drawer-open`).removeClass(`active-right`).removeClass(`drawer-open`)">
        Subscribe
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="log-out-button-mobile">
       <a href="https://mng-prod.auth0.com/v2/logout?returnTo=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.theoaklandpress.com" id="log-out-btn-mobile-a" onclick="$(`.active-right.drawer-open`).removeClass(`active-right`).removeClass(`drawer-open`)">
        Logout
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="log-in-button-mobile" data-mg2-action="login" style="float:right;">
       <a href="https://myaccount.theoaklandpress.com/login.aspx" id="log-in-btn-mobile-a" onclick="$(`.active-right.drawer-open`).removeClass(`active-right`).removeClass(`drawer-open`)">
        Log In
       </a>
      </div>
      <script type="text/javascript">
       (function () {
	'use strict';

	let loginButton = {

		initialize: function () {
			let self = this;
			self.initializeLogin();
		},

		initializeLogin: function () {
			let self = this;
			let pushnavLoginButton = document.querySelectorAll('.log-in-button-mobile')[0];
			let pushnavLoginButtonChild = pushnavLoginButton.querySelector('a');
			let logoutButtonNav = document.getElementsByClassName('log-out-button-mobile')[0];
			let subscribeButton = document.getElementsByClassName('subscribe-button-mobile')[0];

			// add the return params to the subscribe buttons regardless of what happens
			subscribeButtonFlow();

			function loginButtonFlow() {
				pushnavLoginButtonChild.innerHTML = "My Account";
				pushnavLoginButton.removeAttribute("data-mg2-action", "login");
				pushnavLoginButton.style.visibility = "visible";
                //subscribeButton.style.display = "none";
                subscribeButton.style.setProperty("display", "none", "important");

			//	loginButtonChild.innerHTML = "My Account";
			//	loginButton.removeAttribute("data-mg2-action", "login");
			//	loginButton.style.visibility = "visible";
			}

			function subscribeButtonFlow() {
				// do a sanity check to make sure these buttons aren't undefined before we run our script
			//	if ( 'undefined' !== typeof subscribeButton ) {
			//		subscribeParams( subscribeButton );
			//	}
			//	if ( 'undefined' !== typeof pushnavSubscribeButton ) {
			//		subscribeParams( pushnavSubscribeButton );
			//	}
			}

			// function to add some referer params to the subscribe buttons
			function subscribeParams( button ) {

				let button_a;
				let button_href;
				let url;

				// we need to keep this as an object
				button_a = button.getElementsByTagName('a')[0];
				// href string
				button_href = button_a.href;
				// use the url to make some changes
				url = new URL( button_href );
				// append searchparams to the url
				url.searchParams.append( 'returnUrl', window.location.href );
				// set the url attribute with the search params above
				button_a.setAttribute( 'href', url.href );
			}

			function logoutButtonFlow() {
				logoutButtonNav.style.visibility = 'visible';
                subscribeButton.style.setProperty("display", "none", "important");
			//	logoutButton.style.visibility = 'visible';
			//	logoutButtonFooter.style.visibility = 'visible';
			}

			document.addEventListener(
				"onFinish",
				function (e) {
					let mngSubState = Connext.Storage.GetUserState();
					if (mngSubState != "Subscribed") {
					//	pushnavSubscribeButton.style.display = "block";
					//	subscribeButton.style.display = "block";
					} else {
					//	pushnavSubscribeButton.style.display = "none";
					//	subscribeButton.style.display = "none";
					}

					if (mngSubState === "Logged Out") {
						pushnavLoginButton.setAttribute("data-mg2-action", "login");
						pushnavLoginButton.style.visibility = "visible";
                        subscribeButton.style.setProperty("display", "block", "important");   
				//		loginButton.setAttribute("data-mg2-action", "login");
				//		loginButton.style.visibility = "visible";
					} else {
						loginButtonFlow();
					}
				}
			);

			document.addEventListener(
				"onLoggedIn",
				function (e) {
					loginButtonFlow();
					logoutButtonFlow();
				}
			);

			document.addEventListener(
				"onLoginSuccess",
				function (e) {
					loginButtonFlow();
					logoutButtonFlow();
					pushnavLoginButton.style.display = "block";
                    subscribeButton.style.setProperty("display", "block", "important");
				//	loginButton.style.display = "block";
				}
			);

			document.addEventListener(
				'onHasAccess',
				function (e) {
					logoutButtonFlow();
				}
			);

			if ('undefined' !== typeof logoutButtonNav) {
				logoutButtonNav.addEventListener(
					'click',
					function (e) {
						try {
							if (typeof Connext !== 'undefined') {
								e.preventDefault();
								let link = document.querySelector('.log-out-button > a').href;
								Connext.Logout();
								setTimeout(function () {
									window.open(link, '_self');
								}, 2000);
							}
						} catch (e) {
							console.log(e);
						}
					}
				);
			}
		},
	};

	loginButton.initialize();

})();
      </script>
     </div>

           <a href="https://checkout.theoaklandpress.com/?g2i_source=website&amp;g2i_medium=link&amp;g2i_campaign=nav&amp;g2i_or_o=Internet&amp;g2i_or_p=nav">

          <script type="text/javascript">
           /* jshint camelcase: false */
(function () {
	'use strict';

	let loginButton = {

		initialize: function () {
			let self = this;
			self.initializeLogin();
		},

		initializeLogin: function () {
			let self = this;
			let pushnavLoginButton = document.querySelectorAll('.log-in-button')[0];
			let pushnavLoginButtonChild = pushnavLoginButton.querySelector('a');
			//let loginButton = document.querySelectorAll('.log-in-button')[1];
			//let loginButtonChild = loginButton.querySelector('a');
			//let pushnavSubscribeButton = document.querySelectorAll('.tnt-section-subscribe')[0];
			//let subscribeButton = document.querySelectorAll('.tnt-section-subscribe')[4];
                        let subscribeButton = document.getElementsByClassName('subscribe-button')[0];
			let logoutButtonNav = document.getElementsByClassName('log-out-button')[0];
			//let logoutButton = document.getElementsByClassName('log-out-button')[1];
			//let logoutButtonFooter = document.getElementsByClassName('log-out-button')[3];

			// add the return params to the subscribe buttons regardless of what happens
			subscribeButtonFlow();

			function loginButtonFlow() {
				pushnavLoginButtonChild.innerHTML = "My Account";
				pushnavLoginButton.removeAttribute("data-mg2-action", "login");
				pushnavLoginButton.style.visibility = "visible";
                                //subscribeButton.style.display = "none";
                                subscribeButton.style.setProperty("display", "none", "important");

			//	loginButtonChild.innerHTML = "My Account";
			//	loginButton.removeAttribute("data-mg2-action", "login");
			//	loginButton.style.visibility = "visible";
			}

			function subscribeButtonFlow() {
				// do a sanity check to make sure these buttons aren't undefined before we run our script
			//	if ( 'undefined' !== typeof subscribeButton ) {
			//		subscribeParams( subscribeButton );
			//	}
			//	if ( 'undefined' !== typeof pushnavSubscribeButton ) {
			//		subscribeParams( pushnavSubscribeButton );
			//	}
			}

			// function to add some referer params to the subscribe buttons
			function subscribeParams( button ) {

				let button_a;
				let button_href;
				let url;

				// we need to keep this as an object
				button_a = button.getElementsByTagName('a')[0];
				// href string
				button_href = button_a.href;
				// use the url to make some changes
				url = new URL( button_href );
				// append searchparams to the url
				url.searchParams.append( 'returnUrl', window.location.href );
				// set the url attribute with the search params above
				button_a.setAttribute( 'href', url.href );
			}

			function logoutButtonFlow() {
				logoutButtonNav.style.visibility = 'visible';
                                subscribeButton.style.setProperty("display", "none", "important");
			//	logoutButton.style.visibility = 'visible';
			//	logoutButtonFooter.style.visibility = 'visible';
			}

			document.addEventListener(
				"onFinish",
				function (e) {
					let mngSubState = Connext.Storage.GetUserState();
					if (mngSubState != "Subscribed") {
					//	pushnavSubscribeButton.style.display = "block";
					//	subscribeButton.style.display = "block";
					} else {
					//	pushnavSubscribeButton.style.display = "none";
					//	subscribeButton.style.display = "none";
					}

					if (mngSubState === "Logged Out") {
						pushnavLoginButton.setAttribute("data-mg2-action", "login");
						pushnavLoginButton.style.visibility = "visible";
                                                subscribeButton.style.setProperty("display", "block", "important");   
				//		loginButton.setAttribute("data-mg2-action", "login");
				//		loginButton.style.visibility = "visible";
					} else {
						loginButtonFlow();
					}
				}
			);

			document.addEventListener(
				"onLoggedIn",
				function (e) {
					loginButtonFlow();
					logoutButtonFlow();
				}
			);

			document.addEventListener(
				"onLoginSuccess",
				function (e) {
					loginButtonFlow();
					logoutButtonFlow();
					pushnavLoginButton.style.display = "block";
                                        subscribeButton.style.setProperty("display", "block", "important");
				//	loginButton.style.display = "block";
				}
			);

			document.addEventListener(
				'onHasAccess',
				function (e) {
					logoutButtonFlow();
				}
			);

			if ('undefined' !== typeof logoutButtonNav) {
				logoutButtonNav.addEventListener(
					'click',
					function (e) {
						try {
							if (typeof Connext !== 'undefined') {
								e.preventDefault();
								let link = document.querySelector('.log-out-button > a').href;
								Connext.Logout();
								setTimeout(function () {
									window.open(link, '_self');
								}, 2000);
							}
						} catch (e) {
							console.log(e);
						}
					}
				);
			}
		},
	};

	loginButton.initialize();

})();
          </script>

    if ( null !== document.cookie.match(/^(.*;)?\s*auth0.*authenticated.*=.*true.*[^;]+(.*)?$/) ) {

                    <div class="card-lead">
                     <p class="tnt-summary">
                      Division 2, District 9 was held at Allen Park on Saturday, March 20. The top four teams in each district advance to regionals. The Jaguars finished first while Divine Child was second, Auburn Hills Avondale took third and Marysville placed fourth. Check out a recap of the results.
                     </p>
                    </div>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <div class="clearfix">
                  </div>
                 </article>

  <script>
   __tnt.trackEvent = function(obj) {
            if (typeof obj === 'object') {
                    if (obj.category && obj.action) {
                        __tnt.googleEvent(obj);
                    } else if (obj.network && obj.socialAction) {
                        __tnt.googleSocial(obj);
                    } else if (obj.url) {
                        __tnt.googlePageView(obj);
                    }
                    if (typeof TNCMS.Tracking != 'undefined' && obj.metric) {
                        TNCMS.Tracking.addEvent({
                            app: obj.app,
                            metric: obj.metric,
                            id: obj.uuid
                        });
                    }
            }
        };

        if (__tnt.trackEventLater.length > 0) {
            __tnt.trackEventLater.forEach(function(obj) {
                __tnt.trackEvent(obj);
            });
        }

        Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('body [data-track]')).forEach(function(el) {
            el.addEventListener(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function() {
                __tnt.trackEvent(JSON.parse(el.dataset.track));
            });
        });
        Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('body [data-tncms-track-event]')).forEach(function(el) {
            el.addEventListener(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function() {
                __tnt.trackEvent(JSON.parse(el.dataset.tncmsTrackEvent));
            });
        });
        
        Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('body [data-tncms-track-dmp]')).forEach(function(el) {
            el.addEventListener(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function() {
                var dmpData = el.dataset.tncmsTrackDmp;
                
            });
        });
  </script>
  <script>
   /*<![CDATA[*/ 
                __tnt.googleEvent = function(obj) {
                    dataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'tncms.event.trigger',
                             'tncms.event.trigger.category': obj.category,
                             'tncms.event.trigger.action': obj.action,
                             'tncms.event.trigger.label': obj.label, 
                             'tncms.event.trigger.value': obj.value
                    });
                }
                /* Virtual page view */
                __tnt.googlePageView = function(obj) {
                    var sURL = obj.url.replace(/^.*\/\/[^\/]+/, '');
                    dataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'tncms.event.virtual_pageview',
                            'tncms.event.virtual_pageview.url': sURL,
                            'tncms.event.virtual_pageview.title': obj.title
                    });
                }
                /* Social event */
                __tnt.googleSocial = function(obj) {
                    dataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'tncms.event.social',
                            'tncms.event.social.network': obj.network,
                            'tncms.event.social.action': obj.socialAction,
                            'tncms.event.social.target': obj.url
                    });
                } /*]]>*/
  </script>
